 isse 50 lakh se adhik atirikt kaamgaar ipiefo dwaara sanchalit saamaajik suraksha yojanaon ke daayre main aa jaaenge

 paraamarsh ke liye do maheene kaa notice dene ke baad ek adhisuchana ke jariye nunatam seemaa main badlaav kaa ek praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 "now, the Ministry of Labor has planned to go ahead with such amendments to labor laws that do not require parliament's approval
" ham agle maheene ke pratham saptaah tak paraamarsh ke liye notice jari karenge

 The 183rd meeting of the CBD approved the minimum limit for coverage of establishments under the law to be reduced from 50 in case of cooperative institutions to 20 in case of other establishments
